<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 100%; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><tr style="vertical-align: top">
<td style="width: 10%"><b>Item&#160;8.01.</b></td><td style="text-align: justify; width: 90%"><b>Other Events.</b></td></tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On January&#160;7, 2025,
Plains All American Pipeline, L.P. (&#8220;PAA&#8221; or the &#8220;Registrant&#8221;) issued a press release announcing three bolt-on
acquisitions, the purchase of approximately 18% of its outstanding Series&#160;A Preferred Units and a 20% increase in its annualized
distribution rate. A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<tr style="vertical-align: top">

<DOCUMENT>
<TYPE>EX-99.1
<SEQUENCE>2
<FILENAME>tm252840d1_ex99-1.htm
<DESCRIPTION>EXHIBIT 99.1
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><IMG SRC="tm252840d1_ex99-1img001.jpg" ALT=""></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Plains All American Announces Bolt-on Acquisitions,<BR>
Capital Structure Optimization&nbsp;&amp; Distribution Increase</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">HOUSTON &ndash; January&nbsp;7, 2025 &ndash;
Plains All American Pipeline, L.P. (Nasdaq: <U>PAA</U>) and Plains GP Holdings (Nasdaq: <U>PAGP</U>) (collectively, &ldquo;Plains&rdquo;)
announced today three bolt-on acquisitions for an aggregate cash consideration of approximately $670 million net to Plains, the purchase
of approximately 18% of its outstanding PAA Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units and a 20% increase in its annualized distribution rate.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Bolt-on Acquisitions</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Plains signed a definitive agreement to acquire Ironwood Midstream Energy, which owns an Eagle Ford Basin
gathering system, from EnCap Flatrock Midstream for approximately $475 million. The transaction is expected to close in the first quarter
of 2025 following satisfaction of customary closing conditions.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Effective January&nbsp;1, 2025, a subsidiary of Plains Permian Basin joint venture, Plains Oryx Permian
Basin LLC, acquired Medallion Midstream&rsquo;s Delaware Basin crude oil gathering business from The Energy&nbsp;&amp; Minerals Group
for approximately $160 million ($105 million net to PAA&rsquo;s interest).</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">On December&nbsp;23, 2024, a subsidiary of Plains acquired the remaining 50% interest in Midway Pipeline
LLC from a subsidiary of CVR Energy for approximately $90 million.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">These transactions further enhance Plains&rsquo; crude oil footprint in the Permian, Eagle Ford and Mid-Con
at returns consistent with our bolt-on framework and provide incremental return of capital opportunities for our unitholders.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Capital Structure Optimization</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">Plains has also agreed to purchase approximately 12.7 million units, or 18%, of its outstanding Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Units at &ldquo;par&rdquo; ($26.25) for a purchase price of approximately $330 million (plus accrued and unpaid distributions)
from EnCap Flatrock Midstream. This transaction is expected to close in late January&nbsp;2025.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">After giving effect to all of these transactions, Plains' leverage ratio is expected to be at or below
the low-end of our target range of 3.25x to 3.75x, continuing to provide significant balance sheet optionality and flexibility.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Return of Capital Update</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="text-align: justify">The Plains Board of Directors has approved an increase in the quarterly distribution payable in February&nbsp;2025
for both PAA common units and PAGP Class&nbsp;A shares from $0.3175 per unit to $0.38 per unit. On an annualized basis, the distribution
represents a $0.25 per unit, or 20%, increase from the distribution paid in November&nbsp;2024.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&ldquo;The bolt-on acquisitions announced today
are an excellent strategic fit for Plains and allow us to progress our efficient growth strategy by adding high-quality assets adjacent
to our existing integrated footprint,&rdquo; said Willie Chiang, Chairman and CEO of Plains.&nbsp;&ldquo;Importantly, these transactions
create immediate value by delivering sustainable accretion to earnings, distributable cash flow and accelerating return of capital to
unitholders. Our capital allocation framework remains intact, and we remain committed to financial flexibility, capital discipline, generating
meaningful free cash flow and increasing return of capital to our unitholders as demonstrated today.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&#160;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&#160;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>About Plains</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">PAA is a publicly traded master limited partnership
that owns and operates midstream energy infrastructure and provides logistics services for crude oil and natural gas liquids (NGL). PAA
owns an extensive network of pipeline gathering and transportation systems, in addition to terminalling, storage, processing, fractionation
and other infrastructure assets serving key producing basins, transportation corridors and major market hubs and export outlets in the
United States and Canada. On average, PAA handles approximately eight million barrels per day of crude oil and NGL.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">PAGP is a publicly traded entity that owns an
indirect, non-economic controlling general partner interest in PAA and an indirect limited partner interest in PAA, one of the largest
energy infrastructure and logistics companies in North America.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">PAA and PAGP are headquartered in Houston, Texas.
More information is available at <U>www.plains.com</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>Investor Relations Contacts:</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Blake Fernandez</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">Michael Gladstein</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><U>plainsIR@plains.com</U></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">(866) 809-1291</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"></P>
